17.1. Test Framework
ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°: ĞšĞ°ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ»ĞµĞ³ĞºĞ¾Ğ²ĞµÑĞ½Ğ°Ñ Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ

TestRunner.js
javascript

  constructor();
  registerSuite(suite: TestSuite);
  run(filter?: string): Promise<TestResults>;
  runSuite(suiteName: string): Promise<TestResults>;
  onProgress(callback: Function);
  onComplete(callback: Function);
}

TestSuite.js
javascript
class TestSuite {
  constructor(name: string, description?: string);
  beforeAll(fn: Function);
  afterAll(fn: Function);
  beforeEach(fn: Function);
  afterEach(fn: Function);
  test(name: string, fn: Function);
  skip(name: string, fn: Function);
  only(name: string, fn: Function);
}

Assert.js
javascript
class Assert {
  static equal(actual, expected, message?);
  static notEqual(actual, expected, message?);
  static strictEqual(actual, expected, message?);
  static deepEqual(actual, expected, message?);
  static throws(fn, error?, message?);
  static doesNotThrow(fn, message?);
  static isTrue(value, message?);
  static isFalse(value, message?);
  static isNull(value, message?);
  static isNotNull(value, message?);
  static isDefined(value, message?);
  static isUndefined(value, message?);
  static instanceOf(obj, constructor, message?);
  static match(string, regex, message?);
}

MockFactory.js
javascript

class MockFactory {
  static createMock(object);
  static createSpy(name?);
  static stub(object, method, implementation?);
  static restore(object, method?);
}

class Spy {
  called: boolean;
  callCount: number;
  calls: Array<{ args, returnValue, timestamp }>;
  
  mockReturnValue(value);
  mockImplementation(fn);
  reset();
}

17.3. Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° Ñ‚ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ°
Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ½:

javascript
// tests/unit/core/signals.test.js
import { TestSuite } from '../../test-framework/TestSuite.js';
import { Assert } from '../../test-framework/Assert.js';
import { Signal } from '../../../src/core/signals/Signal.js';

const suite = new TestSuite('Signal', 'Reactive signals implementation');

suite.beforeEach(() => {
  // Setup
});

suite.afterEach(() => {
  // Cleanup
});

suite.test('should create signal with initial value', () => {
  const signal = new Signal(42);
  Assert.equal(signal.value, 42);
});

suite.test('should notify subscribers on value change', () => {
  const signal = new Signal(0);
  let notified = false;
  
  signal.subscribe(() => {
    notified = true;
  });
  
  signal.value = 10;
  
  Assert.isTrue(notified);
});

export default suite;
